GT Equivalence Verification (MatSci6)
============================================================
GT: c0*epsilon*(-c1*(T - c2) + c3) + epsilon*c4*(T - c5)**c6
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is a fixed polynomial in \(T\) times \(\epsilon\), with a shared shift \(a=342.5784399345082\):
\[
\text{GT}=\epsilon\Big(21.698090453033654\big(1-0.05460334940892902(T-a)\big)+5.6497230214391285(T-a)^2\Big).
\]
So GT has these structural properties:

- **Overall factor \(\epsilon\)** (so GT \(=0\) for all \(T\) when \(\epsilon=0\)).
- **Quadratic in \(T\)** (after expansion): \(\epsilon(\alpha T^2+\beta T+\gamma)\) with fixed \(\alpha,\beta,\gamma\).
- **No** \(\epsilon^2,\epsilon^3\), no \(|\epsilon|\), no logs/exps/sin/cos, no piecewise (Max), no denominators in \(T\).

A candidate can match only if it can be reduced (by choosing its constants) to exactly \(\epsilon(\alpha T^2+\beta T+\gamma)\) for all \((\epsilon,T)\).

---

### 1
Has \(T^2 c0\epsilon/(T+c1)\) (rational in \(T\)), plus \(T c2\) (not multiplied by \(\epsilon\)), plus \(\exp(c4\epsilon)\), constants, and \((c8|\epsilon|+1)^{c9}\). Cannot become a pure polynomial \(\epsilon(\cdot)\) for all \(T,\epsilon\). **No match**.

### 2
Form: \(T c0\epsilon + (c1+c3)\epsilon + c2 + c4\epsilon^3 + c5(\cdots|\epsilon|\cdots)\).
To match GT: need \(c2=0\), kill \(\epsilon^3\) (set \(c4=0\)), kill \(|\epsilon|\) term (set \(c5=0\)). Then left is only linear in \(T\): \(\epsilon(c0 T + \text{const})\), but GT is quadratic in \(T\). **No match**.

### 3
Has \(T c0\epsilon\) plus \(\log(c4\epsilon^5+1)\) and \((c6\epsilon+1)^{c7}\) terms not representable as \(\epsilon\) times quadratic in \(T\) for all \(\epsilon\). Also has additive constant \(c2\) unless zero. Even if those are zeroed, only linear in \(T\). **No match**.

### 4
Has \(T c0\epsilon\) plus \(c3\epsilon^{c4}\, \max(0,Tc5+1)^{c6}\) (piecewise in \(T\), nonlinear in \(\epsilon\)). Cannot equal a global polynomial in \(T\) for all \(T\). **No match**.

### 5
Logs and \((Tc7+1)^{c8}\) and \(|\epsilon|^{c9}\). Not reducible to \(\epsilon\) times quadratic polynomial in \(T\) globally. **No match**.

### 6
Contains \(\exp(c1\epsilon)\), \(\cos(Tc3)\), \(\exp(Tc5)\cos(Tc6)\), and \((c8\epsilon+1)^{c9}\). Cannot become polynomial in \(T\) for all \(T\). **No match**.

### 7
Has exponentials in \(\epsilon\), rational in \(T\) term \((Tc7+1)^{-5}\), \(|\epsilon|\) power. Not polynomial. **No match**.

### 8
Has \(\exp\) inside log with \(T\) in exponent, and \(\max(0,Tc8+1)^{c9}\). Not polynomial. **No match**.

### 9
Only depends on \(\epsilon\) (no \(T\)). GT depends on \(T\). **No match**.

### 10
Has \((Tc5+1)^{-5}\) rational in \(T\) and \(|\epsilon|\). Not polynomial. **No match**.

### 11
Has terms \(T c0 + T c1\) not multiplied by \(\epsilon\), plus \(\exp(c3\epsilon)\), plus \((c6|\epsilon|+1)^5\). Cannot enforce overall factor \(\epsilon\) for all \(T,\epsilon\). **No match**.

### 12
Has \(\exp(Tc6)\log(c7\epsilon+1)\) (non-polynomial in \(T\)). **No match**.

### 13
Has \(T c0\) (no \(\epsilon\)), \(T c1(\epsilon+1)^5\), \(\exp(c4\epsilon)\), \(|\epsilon|\) power. Cannot reduce to \(\epsilon\) times quadratic polynomial in \(T\). **No match**.

### 14
Has \(c2/(c3\epsilon+1)^5\) and \(\exp(c5\log(Tc6+1)\log(\cdot))\). Not polynomial. **No match**.

### 15
Form: \(T c0\epsilon + T c1 + T c2\exp(c3\epsilon) + c4 + (c5+c6)\epsilon\).
To match GT need \(T c1\) vanish (\(c1=0\)), constant \(c4=0\), exponential term vanish (\(c2=0\)). Left is linear in \(T\): \(\epsilon(c0 T + \text{const})\). GT is quadratic in \(T\). **No match**.

### 16
Has \((T+1)^{c8}\log(c9\epsilon^2+1)\) and \((c5|\epsilon|+1)^{c6}\) and \(\exp(c2\epsilon)\). Not polynomial. **No match**.

### 17
Has \(T c0(\epsilon+1)^5\), \(\epsilon\log(\cdot)\), \(\log(Tc5+1)\log(\cdot)\), and Max. Not polynomial. **No match**.

### 18
Has \(T^2 c0\epsilon\) and \(T c1\epsilon\) (good), but also \(T c2(\epsilon+1)^{c3}\) and \(T c4\) (no \(\epsilon\)), plus \(\epsilon e^{c6\epsilon}\) and \(\log(Tc8+1)\log(\cdot)\). To match GT would need to kill all non-polynomial/non-\(\epsilon\)-factored terms: set \(c2=0\), \(c4=0\), \(c5=0\), \(c7=0\). Then candidate becomes \(\epsilon(c0 T^2 + c1 T)\) with **no \(\epsilon\) constant term**; GT has a nonzero \(\epsilon\cdot\gamma\). No way to add \(\epsilon\gamma\) without reintroducing forbidden structure. **No match**.

### 19
Form: \(T c0\epsilon + (c1+c3)\epsilon + c2 + c4\epsilon^{c5} + c6\epsilon(Tc7+1)^{c8}\).
To match GT need \(c2=0\). The last term is \(\epsilon\) times \((Tc7+1)^{c8}\); to be polynomial quadratic in \(T\) for all \(T\), would need \(c8\in\{0,1,2\}\) and expand, but it’s a power of an affine term; if \(c8=2\), gives \(\epsilon\) times quadratic in \(T\) **but with fixed relationship between \(T^2,T,\)const coefficients** (they must satisfy binomial proportions). GT’s coefficients are arbitrary (not constrained to binomial form). Also there is already a separate \(T c0\epsilon\) and \(\epsilon\) constant, which would break the binomial constraint unless carefully combined—still the combined quadratic would generally not be representable as \(A(Tb+1)^2 + CT + D\) with free parameters? Actually it would be representable as general quadratic if we allow independent \(T^2,T,\)const coefficients; but here \(T^2\) comes only from that powered term, and its \(T\) and const parts are tied to it. Adding extra \(T\epsilon\) and \(\epsilon\) constants can free the \(T\) and const coefficients, but **the \(T^2\) coefficient then forces a specific \(T\) coefficient contribution from the same term that must be canceled/adjusted by \(T c0\epsilon\)**—that is possible. However the \(\epsilon^{c5}\) term must become linear in \(\epsilon\): set \(c5=1\) and fold into \(\epsilon\) constant, or set \(c4=0\). Even then, the quadratic is of form:
\[
\epsilon\big( (c6 c7^2)T^2 + (c0 + 2c6 c7)T + (c1+c3+c6)\big)
\]
(if \(c8=2\)). This is a fully general quadratic in \(T\) because \(c6,c7\) control \(T^2\) and part of \(T\), and \(c0\) can adjust \(T\) independently, and constants adjust constant term. So **in principle** it could match GT’s \(\alpha,\beta,\gamma\). But there is a catch: \(T^2\) coefficient is \(c6 c7^2\) which must be \(\alpha\) (nonzero), so \(c6\neq 0\). Then the induced \(T\) coefficient contribution \(2c6 c7\) can be any real by choosing \(c7\) sign/magnitude, and \(c0\) can finish matching. Constant term also adjustable. Therefore candidate 19 **can** represent any \(\epsilon(\alpha T^2+\beta T+\gamma)\). So **this one matches**.

### 20
Has \(T^2 c0\epsilon + T c1\epsilon\) plus \(T c2\) (no \(\epsilon\)), plus \(\epsilon e^{c4\epsilon}\), plus log products. To match GT must set \(c2=0\), \(c3=0\), \(c5=0\), leaving \(\epsilon(c0 T^2 + c1 T + c8)\). This can match GT’s quadratic (choose \(c0,c1,c8\)). Yes: set \(c0=\alpha\), \(c1=\beta\), \(c8=\gamma\). **Match**.

### 21
Has \(T^2 c0\epsilon + T c1\epsilon + (c2+c4)\epsilon + c3 +\) log term depending on \(T\) and \(\epsilon\). Need \(c3=0\) and kill log term (\(c5=0\)). Then becomes \(\epsilon(c0 T^2 + c1 T + \text{const})\), which can match GT. **Match**.

### 22
Has log terms and \(\log(c8 e^{c9\epsilon}+1)\) (nonlinear in \(\epsilon\)) unless killed. Set \(c4=0\), \(c7=0\), and also \(c2=0\) to remove \(\epsilon e^{c3\epsilon}\) unless \(c3=0\) and it becomes linear \(\epsilon\) (could keep). After killing, can reduce to \(\epsilon(c0 T^2 + c1 T + \text{const})\). **Match** (e.g., set \(c2\) with \(c3=0\) to supply constant-in-\(T\) \(\epsilon\) term, or just use \(c2=0\) and add via other constant if present—here none besides that, so keep \(c2\neq0,c3=0\) to get \(c2\epsilon\)).

### 23
Has \(c2 e^{c3|\epsilon|}\) (nonlinear in \(\epsilon\)) and constant \(c9\). To match GT need \(c2=0\), \(c6=0\), \(c9=0\). Remaining \(T^2 c0\epsilon + T c1\epsilon + c4\epsilon e^{c5\epsilon}\). Set \(c5=0\) so \(e^{0}=1\), giving \(c4\epsilon\). Then \(\epsilon(c0 T^2 + c1 T + c4)\) matches GT. **Match**.

### 24
Form: \(\epsilon(c0 T^2 + c1 T) + T c2\epsilon^3 + c3\epsilon e^{c4\epsilon}\).
Need kill \(\epsilon^3\) term: \(c2=0\). Make last term linear in \(\epsilon\): set \(c4=0\) so it is \(c3\epsilon\). Then \(\epsilon(c0 T^2 + c1 T + c3)\) matches GT. **Match**.

### 25
Has log product and \(e^{c8\epsilon}\log(|\epsilon|)\) type; must set \(c4=0\) and \(c7=0\). Then left \(T^2 c0\epsilon + T c1\epsilon + c2\epsilon e^{c3\epsilon}\). Set \(c3=0\) to make \(c2\epsilon\). Then matches. **Match**.

### 26
Has \(c7 e^{c8/T}|\epsilon|\) (non-polynomial and \(|\epsilon|\)); must set \(c7=0\). Also set \(c4=0\). Then reduce as in 25: set \(c3=0\) to get constant \(\epsilon\) term. **Match**.

### 27
Has \(c7\epsilon e^{T c8}\) (non-polynomial in \(T\)); set \(c7=0\). Also set \(c4=0\). Then reduce to \(\epsilon(c0 T^2 + c1 T + c2)\) by setting \(c3=0\). **Match**.

### 28
Has log product; set \(c4=0\). Then \(T^2 c0\epsilon + T c1\epsilon + c2\epsilon e^{c3\epsilon}\). Set \(c3=0\) to get \(c2\epsilon\). **Match**.

### 29
